upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati adinnaṃ ādiyati musā bhaṇati pisuṇaṃ bhaṇati pharusaṃ bhaṇatisamphaṃ palapati sandhiṃ chindati nillopaṃ harati ekāgārikaṃ karoti paripanthe tiṭṭhati paradāraṃ gacchati gāmaghātaṃ karoti nigamaghātaṃ karoti mātaraṃ pitaraṃPañhavāro                          arahantaṃ jīvitā voropeti duṭṭhena cittena Tathāgatassa lohitaṃ uppādeti saṅghaṃ bhindati  Kāyikaṃ dukkhaṃutuṃ
